<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sьde</i> (Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">сьде</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sĭde</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">zdè</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">zde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***здешний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здешний.html>зде́шний</a> (3537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зде(сь)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zde(sʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здешний.html>зде́шний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdéšnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> local, relating to this place (the place where the speaker is currently located)
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Марко <a href = vnd.unilang:полый.html>По́ло</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>Книга</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразие.html>разнообра́зии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></i> c. 1300:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старину́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:здешний.html>зде́шние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворянин.html>дворя́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́бры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинственный.html>вои́нственны</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v starinú <b>zdéšnije</b> dvorjáne býli xrábry i voínstvenny</i></dd><dd>in the old times <b>local</b> nobles were courageous and combative</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровающийся.html>здоро́вающийся</a> (6377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровающийся.html>здоро́вающийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdoróvajuščijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здороваться.html>здоро́ваться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdoróvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́во</a> (1794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здо́рово</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdórovo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> great, very well, awesomely</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very strongly, to a very great extent</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is great, it is awesome, it is cool
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b>,  Arkady Strugatsky and Boris Strugatsky,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>Тру́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гом</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здо́рово</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрела́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проволока.html>про́волоку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́м</a> а́нки.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Býlo by <b>zdórovo</b>, jésli by strelá perebíla próvoloku, i znak upál by prjámo k nogám Ánki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It would be <b>awesome</b> if the arrow broke the wire and the sign fell right at Anka's feet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***здоровый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́вый</a> (1012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъdorvъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdrávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdoróvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)здорове́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)здорове́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>healthy, sound</li>
<li>strong, robust</li>
<li>wholesome, salubrious</li>
<li>big, large</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdoróvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ье</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdoróvʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вий</a></b>)

<ol><li>health
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ше</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za váše <b>zdoróvʹje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to your health, here’s to you (toast)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>zdoróvʹje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to your heart’s content; you're welcome</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***здравствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здравствовать.html>здра́вствовать</a> (1408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdrávyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">healthy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ствовать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравствовать.html>здра́вствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdrávstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (the first <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is not pronounced)
</p>
<ol><li>to be well, to prosper, to thrive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здравствовать.html>здра́вствует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:король.html>коро́ль</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">da zdrávstvujet korólʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">long live the king!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***здравый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a> (5449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">съдравъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭdravŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zdoróvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited Old East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdrávyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)здра́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)здра́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sensible, sound, sane, reasonable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смысл.html>смысл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdrávyj smysl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">common sense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:здравый.html>здра́вом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уме́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>zdrávom</b> umé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sane, in one's right mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> healthy</li></ol>

***зевака.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́ка</a> (10786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевать.html>зева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zevátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zeváka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>idler, gaper, gawker, spectator; person who is primarily busy looking at something for fun, and without a particular purpose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уличный.html>у́личный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фокусник.html>фо́кусник</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зевака.html>зева́к</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Úličnyj fókusnik sobrál tolpú <b>zevák</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Street magician gathered a crowd.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***зевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зевать.html>зева́ть</a> (7397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zěvati</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">зіва́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ziváty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Russian Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">зѣвати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zěvati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">зиjѐвати</i> (first singular <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">зи̏jева̑м</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">zévati</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">zívati</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ziewać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">zywać</i>. Also cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зиять.html>зия́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zijátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">žióvauti</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">žàvât</i>, as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">giwēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gewōn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевать.html>зева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевнуть.html>зевну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прозевать.html>прозева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to yawn
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевнуть.html>зевну́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zevnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss (a train, a stop, a chance, an opportunity, etc.)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прозевать.html>прозева́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prozevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:терять.html>теря́ть</a> что-либо из-за невнимательности <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глазеть.html>глазе́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зевок.html>зево́к</a> (30330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевать.html>зева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевок.html>зево́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zevók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевок.html>зевка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевок.html>зевки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевок.html>зевко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>yawn</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> temporary loss of vigilance <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually leading to negative results</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***зеленеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зеленеть.html>зелене́ть</a> (10209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>зелёный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zeljónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленеть.html>зелене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zelenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позеленеть.html>позелене́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become, turn green
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленеть.html>зелене́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зависть.html>за́висти</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ревность.html>ре́вности</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zelenétʹ</b> ot závisti (révnosti)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn/be green with envy (jealousy)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to show green</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зазеленеть.html>зазелене́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zazelenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позеленеть.html>позелене́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pozelenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зелье.html>зе́лье</a> (14188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zelьje</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зелье.html>зе́лье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zélʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зелье.html>зе́лья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зелье.html>зе́лья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зелье.html>зе́лий</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земля́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zemljá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земельный.html>земе́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zemélʹnyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> land; agricultural
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:земельный.html>земе́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:реформа.html>рефо́рма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zemélʹnaja</b> refórma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">land reform</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:земельный.html>земе́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:участок.html>уча́сток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zemélʹnyj</b> učástok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">plot of land</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***земледельческий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:земледельческий.html>земледе́льческий</a> (22405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">земледе́л(ие)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zemledél(ije)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-českij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земледельческий.html>земледе́льческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zemledélʹčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> farming</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
